## 1: Prompt 1

Optimize the substrate kernel in /workspace/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb1/p01/optimization_rounds/round2/output_model_new.py

Use MFMA instructions `S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32` to do matrix multiplications and loads the data from global memory using vectorized loads S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4. The MFMA instruction computes 32x32x8 matmul cooperatively in a wave. Build larger tiles by issuing multiple MFMA instructions across K and output subtiles.
  
MFMA swizzle invariants:
  For A, `i in [0,32)`, `j in [0,8)`: `A(i, j) -> (lane_id = i + (j / 4) * 32, element = j % 4)`
  For B, `j in [0,8)`, `i in [0,32)`: `B(j, i) -> (lane_id = j + (i / 4) * 32, element = i % 4)`

Accumulator invariant for C: for each lane in [0, 64) and acc_idx in [0, 16):
  - col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
  - row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)

Do not invent a different unpacking. Do not use a naive acc_idx -> contiguous row mapping. Treat this mapping as fixed when writing results.

Stage A and B through LDS. Each thread loads operand fragments in 16-byte chunks. Treat each 16-byte fragment as `(4, S.u32)` and reinterpret it as `2 x (4, S.bf16)`. Feed both `(4, S.bf16)` halves into MFMA in natural order. The intended effect is a cooperative `32x32x16` accumulation from two natural MFMA steps. Do not add lane-dependent or K-dependent control flow to select halves.
  - The two `(4, S.bf16)` halves from one 16-byte LDS load collectively represent a swizzled `32x16` operand contribution with 4-column interleaving.
  - Consuming them in natural order must produce the same final C as a naive conceptual layout because operand pairings remain consistent under MFMA swizzle.

Scale the kernel from one wave to four waves without changing the MFMA per-wave invariant. Interpret the 4 warps as a 2 x 2 warp grid. Keep MFMA math identical per warp. Only add warp ownership offsets at operand fetch and output writeback.

import torch
import torch.nn as nn

import substrate
import substrate.language as S


N = 4096
BLOCK_M = 64
BLOCK_N = 64
WAVE_SIZE = 64
WAVES_M = 2
WAVES_N = 2
BLOCK_THREADS = WAVE_SIZE * WAVES_M * WAVES_N
K_CHUNK = 16
K_TILES = N // K_CHUNK
RANGE_BYTES = N * N * 2


@substrate.jit
def gemm_kernel(
    A: S.Tensor((N, N), S.bf16),
    B: S.Tensor((N, N), S.bf16),
    C: S.Tensor((N, N), S.bf16),
):
    tid = S.thread_id(0)
    wave_id = tid >> 6
    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
    warp_row = wave_id >> 1
    warp_col = wave_id % 2

    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
    tile_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
    tile_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32

    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, S.convert(RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B, S.convert(RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))

    # Per-wave swizzled LDS staging buffers. Each row is one 16-byte fragment.
    a_smem = S.make_shared((4 * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
    b_smem = S.make_shared((4 * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
    acc = S.make_local((16,), S.f32)
    frag_layout = S.make_layout((2, 4), (4, 1))
    b_lane_layout = S.make_layout((4 * 64, 8), (8, 1))
    b_smem_bf16 = S.view(b_smem, S.bf16, b_lane_layout)

    for i in S.range(16):
        acc[i] = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)

    for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
        k_base = k_tile * K_CHUNK

        a_row = lane >> 1
        a_half = lane & 1
        a_byte_off = ((tile_row_base + a_row) * N + k_base + a_half * 8) * 2
        a_words = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_byte_off, S.i32), 0)

        a_base0 = (wave_id * 64 + a_row) * 4 + a_half * 2
        a_base1 = (wave_id * 64 + a_row + 32) * 4 + a_half * 2
        a_smem[a_base0] = a_words[0]
        a_smem[a_base0 + 1] = a_words[1]
        a_smem[a_base1] = a_words[2]
        a_smem[a_base1 + 1] = a_words[3]

        b_k = lane >> 2
        b_col_frag = lane & 3
        b_byte_off = ((k_base + b_k) * N + tile_col_base + b_col_frag * 8) * 2
        b_words = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_byte_off, S.i32), 0)
        b_vals = S.view(b_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
        b_step = b_k >> 3
        b_quarter = (b_k >> 2) & 1
        b_elem = b_k & 3
        b_dst_idx = b_step * 4 + b_elem
        b_lane_base = wave_id * 64 + b_quarter * 32 + b_col_frag * 8
        for s in S.range(4):
            b_smem_bf16[b_lane_base + s, b_dst_idx] = b_vals[0, s, 0]
            b_smem_bf16[b_lane_base + 4 + s, b_dst_idx] = b_vals[1, s, 0]

        S.syncthreads()

        lane_base = (wave_id * 64 + lane) * 4
        a_lane_words = S.subview(a_smem, (lane_base,), (4,), (1,))
        b_lane_words = S.subview(b_smem, (lane_base,), (4,), (1,))
        a_frag = S.view(a_lane_words, S.bf16, frag_layout)
        b_frag = S.view(b_lane_words, S.bf16, frag_layout)

        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)

        S.syncthreads()

    col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
    lane_row_quad = 4 * (lane >> 5)
    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
        row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx >> 2) + lane_row_quad + (acc_idx & 3)
        C[row, col] = S.convert(acc[acc_idx], S.bf16)


class ModelNew(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()

    def forward(self, A: torch.Tensor, B: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
        if tuple(A.shape) != (N, N) or tuple(B.shape) != (N, N):
            raise ValueError(f"expected {(N, N)} inputs, got {tuple(A.shape)} and {tuple(B.shape)}")
        if A.dtype != torch.bfloat16 or B.dtype != torch.bfloat16:
            raise TypeError(f"expected bfloat16 inputs, got {A.dtype} and {B.dtype}")
        if A.device != B.device:
            raise ValueError("A and B must be on the same device")

        A = A.contiguous()
        B = B.contiguous()
        C = torch.empty((N, N), device=A.device, dtype=torch.bfloat16)
        gemm_kernel[lambda: ((N // BLOCK_N, N // BLOCK_M, 1), (BLOCK_THREADS, 1, 1))](A, B, C)
        return C

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import unittest

import torch

import substrate
import substrate.language as S
from substrate.testing import has_rocm


@substrate.jit
def gemm_mfma_16x16x16(
    A: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.u32),
    B: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.u32),
    C: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.f32),
):
    lane = S.thread_id(0)

    c_lane = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.f32)

    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.f16))
    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.f16))

    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_16x16x16_f16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_16x16x16_f16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)

    C[lane] = c_lane


@substrate.jit
def gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16(
    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
):
    lane = S.thread_id(0)

    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)

    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))

    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)

    C[lane] = c_lane

import torch
import torch.nn as nn

import substrate
import substrate.language as S


N = 4096
BLOCK_M = 64
BLOCK_N = 64
WAVE_SIZE = 64
WAVES_M = 2
WAVES_N = 2
BLOCK_THREADS = WAVE_SIZE * WAVES_M * WAVES_N
K_CHUNK = 16
K_TILES = N // K_CHUNK
RANGE_BYTES = N * N * 2


@substrate.jit
def gemm_kernel(
    A: S.Tensor((N, N), S.bf16),
    B: S.Tensor((N, N), S.bf16),
    C: S.Tensor((N, N), S.bf16),
):
    tid = S.thread_id(0)
    wave_id = tid >> 6
    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
    warp_row = wave_id >> 1
    warp_col = wave_id % 2

    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
    tile_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
    tile_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32

    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, S.convert(RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))
    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B, S.convert(RANGE_BYTES, S.i32))

    # Per-wave swizzled LDS staging buffers. Each row is one 16-byte fragment.
    a_smem = S.make_shared((4 * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
    b_smem = S.make_shared((4 * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
    acc = S.make_local((16,), S.f32)
    frag_layout = S.make_layout((2, 4), (4, 1))
    b_lane_layout = S.make_layout((4 * 64, 8), (8, 1))
    b_smem_bf16 = S.view(b_smem, S.bf16, b_lane_layout)

    for i in S.range(16):
        acc[i] = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)

    for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
        k_base = k_tile * K_CHUNK

        a_row = lane >> 1
        a_half = lane & 1
        a_byte_off = ((tile_row_base + a_row) * N + k_base + a_half * 8) * 2
        a_words = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_byte_off, S.i32), 0)

        a_base0 = (wave_id * 64 + a_row) * 4 + a_half * 2
        a_base1 = (wave_id * 64 + a_row + 32) * 4 + a_half * 2
        a_smem[a_base0] = a_words[0]
        a_smem[a_base0 + 1] = a_words[1]
        a_smem[a_base1] = a_words[2]
        a_smem[a_base1 + 1] = a_words[3]

        b_k = lane >> 2
        b_col_frag = lane & 3
        b_byte_off = ((k_base + b_k) * N + tile_col_base + b_col_frag * 8) * 2
        b_words = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_byte_off, S.i32), 0)
        b_vals = S.view(b_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
        b_step = b_k >> 3
        b_quarter = (b_k >> 2) & 1
        b_elem = b_k & 3
        b_dst_idx = b_step * 4 + b_elem
        b_lane_base = wave_id * 64 + b_quarter * 32 + b_col_frag * 8
        for s in S.range(4):
            b_smem_bf16[b_lane_base + s, b_dst_idx] = b_vals[0, s, 0]
            b_smem_bf16[b_lane_base + 4 + s, b_dst_idx] = b_vals[1, s, 0]

        S.syncthreads()

        lane_base = (wave_id * 64 + lane) * 4
        a_lane_words = S.subview(a_smem, (lane_base,), (4,), (1,))
        b_lane_words = S.subview(b_smem, (lane_base,), (4,), (1,))
        a_frag = S.view(a_lane_words, S.bf16, frag_layout)
        b_frag = S.view(b_lane_words, S.bf16, frag_layout)

        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], acc)
        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], acc)

        S.syncthreads()

    col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
    lane_row_quad = 4 * (lane >> 5)
    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
        row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx >> 2) + lane_row_quad + (acc_idx & 3)
        C[row, col] = S.convert(acc[acc_idx], S.bf16)


class ModelNew(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()

    def forward(self, A: torch.Tensor, B: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
        if tuple(A.shape) != (N, N) or tuple(B.shape) != (N, N):
            raise ValueError(f"expected {(N, N)} inputs, got {tuple(A.shape)} and {tuple(B.shape)}")
        if A.dtype != torch.bfloat16 or B.dtype != torch.bfloat16:
            raise TypeError(f"expected bfloat16 inputs, got {A.dtype} and {B.dtype}")
        if A.device != B.device:
            raise ValueError("A and B must be on the same device")

        A = A.contiguous()
        B = B.contiguous()
        C = torch.empty((N, N), device=A.device, dtype=torch.bfloat16)
        gemm_kernel[lambda: ((N // BLOCK_N, N // BLOCK_M, 1), (BLOCK_THREADS, 1, 1))](A, B, C)
        return C

codex
The failure is a compiler typing issue from reusing fragment-view names across stages. I’m making a focused patch to give each stage its own fragment variables and rerunning the same evaluation command.
apply patch

+    even_stage = (final_pair & 1) * LDS_STAGE_WORDS
+    odd_stage = even_stage ^ LDS_STAGE_WORDS

+    a_odd_words = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_odd_byte_off, S.i32), 0)

+    b_odd_vals = S.view(b_odd_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+

+    a_final_even_lane_words = S.subview(a_smem, (lane_base,), (4,), (1,))
+    b_final_even_lane_words = S.subview(b_smem, (lane_base,), (4,), (1,))
+    a_final_even_frag = S.view(a_final_even_lane_words, S.bf16, frag_layout)
+    b_final_even_frag = S.view(b_final_even_lane_words, S.bf16, frag_layout)

+    a_base1 = odd_stage + (wave_id * 64 + a_row + 32) * 4 + a_half * 2
+    a_smem[a_base0] = a_odd_words[0]

+    a_smem[a_base1] = a_odd_words[2]

   123	        a_next_even_words = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_next_even_byte_off, S.i32), 0)
   124	
   125	        b_next_even_byte_off = ((next_even_k_base + b_k) * N + tile_col_base + b_col_frag * 8) * 2
   126	        b_next_even_words = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
   127	            b_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_next_even_byte_off, S.i32), 0
   128	        )
   129	        b_next_even_vals = S.view(b_next_even_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
   130	
   131	        lane_base = odd_stage + (wave_id * 64 + lane) * 4
   132	        a_odd_lane_words = S.subview(a_smem, (lane_base,), (4,), (1,))
   133	        b_odd_lane_words = S.subview(b_smem, (lane_base,), (4,), (1,))
   134	        a_odd_frag = S.view(a_odd_lane_words, S.bf16, frag_layout)
   135	        b_odd_frag = S.view(b_odd_lane_words, S.bf16, frag_layout)
   136	
   137	        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_odd_frag[0], b_odd_frag[0], acc)
   138	
   139	        a_base0 = even_stage + (wave_id * 64 + a_row) * 4 + a_half * 2
   140	        a_base1 = even_stage + (wave_id * 64 + a_row + 32) * 4 + a_half * 2
   141	        a_smem[a_base0] = a_next_even_words[0]
   142	        a_smem[a_base0 + 1] = a_next_even_words[1]
   143	        a_smem[a_base1] = a_next_even_words[2]
   144	        a_smem[a_base1 + 1] = a_next_even_words[3]
   145	        b_lane_base = (even_stage // 4) + wave_id * 64 + b_quarter * 32 + b_col_frag * 8
   146	        for s in S.range(4):
   147	            b_smem_bf16[b_lane_base + s, b_dst_idx] = b_next_even_vals[0, s, 0]
   148	            b_smem_bf16[b_lane_base + 4 + s, b_dst_idx] = b_next_even_vals[1, s, 0]
   149	
   150	        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_odd_frag[1], b_odd_frag[1], acc)
   151	
   152	        S.syncthreads()
   153	
   154	    final_pair = K_TILE_PAIRS - 1
   155	    even_stage = (final_pair & 1) * LDS_STAGE_WORDS
   156	    odd_stage = even_stage ^ LDS_STAGE_WORDS
   157	
   158	    odd_k_base = (final_pair * 2 + 1) * K_CHUNK
   159	    a_odd_byte_off = ((tile_row_base + a_row) * N + odd_k_base + a_half * 8) * 2
   160	    a_odd_words = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_odd_byte_off, S.i32), 0)
   161	
   162	    b_odd_byte_off = ((odd_k_base + b_k) * N + tile_col_base + b_col_frag * 8) * 2
   163	    b_odd_words = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_odd_byte_off, S.i32), 0)
   164	    b_odd_vals = S.view(b_odd_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
   165	
   166	    lane_base = even_stage + (wave_id * 64 + lane) * 4
   167	    a_final_even_lane_words = S.subview(a_smem, (lane_base,), (4,), (1,))
   168	    b_final_even_lane_words = S.subview(b_smem, (lane_base,), (4,), (1,))

   170	    b_final_even_frag = S.view(b_final_even_lane_words, S.bf16, frag_layout)
   171	
   172	    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_final_even_frag[0], b_final_even_frag[0], acc)
   173	
   174	    a_base0 = odd_stage + (wave_id * 64 + a_row) * 4 + a_half * 2
   175	    a_base1 = odd_stage + (wave_id * 64 + a_row + 32) * 4 + a_half * 2
   176	    a_smem[a_base0] = a_odd_words[0]
   177	    a_smem[a_base0 + 1] = a_odd_words[1]
   178	    a_smem[a_base1] = a_odd_words[2]
   179	    a_smem[a_base1 + 1] = a_odd_words[3]
   180	    b_lane_base = (odd_stage // 4) + wave_id * 64 + b_quarter * 32 + b_col_frag * 8
   181	    for s in S.range(4):
   182	        b_smem_bf16[b_lane_base + s, b_dst_idx] = b_odd_vals[0, s, 0]
   183	        b_smem_bf16[b_lane_base + 4 + s, b_dst_idx] = b_odd_vals[1, s, 0]
   184	
   185	    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_final_even_frag[1], b_final_even_frag[1], acc)
   186	
   187	    S.syncthreads()
   188	
   189	    lane_base = odd_stage + (wave_id * 64 + lane) * 4
   190	    a_final_odd_lane_words = S.subview(a_smem, (lane_base,), (4,), (1,))
   191	    b_final_odd_lane_words = S.subview(b_smem, (lane_base,), (4,), (1,))
   192	    a_final_odd_frag = S.view(a_final_odd_lane_words, S.bf16, frag_layout)
   193	    b_final_odd_frag = S.view(b_final_odd_lane_words, S.bf16, frag_layout)
   194	
   195	    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_final_odd_frag[0], b_final_odd_frag[0], acc)
   196	    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_final_odd_frag[1], b_final_odd_frag[1], acc)
   197	
   198	    col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
   199	    lane_row_quad = 4 * (lane >> 5)
   200	    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
   201	        row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx >> 2) + lane_row_quad + (acc_idx & 3)
   202	        C[row, col] = S.convert(acc[acc_idx], S.bf16)
   203	
   204	
   205	class ModelNew(nn.Module):
   206	    def __init__(self):
   207	        super().__init__()
   208	
   209	    def forward(self, A: torch.Tensor, B: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
   210	        if tuple(A.shape) != (N, N) or tuple(B.shape) != (N, N):
   211	            raise ValueError(f"expected {(N, N)} inputs, got {tuple(A.shape)} and {tuple(B.shape)}")
   212	        if A.dtype != torch.bfloat16 or B.dtype != torch.bfloat16:
   213	            raise TypeError(f"expected bfloat16 inputs, got {A.dtype} and {B.dtype}")
   214	        if A.device != B.device:
   215	            raise ValueError("A and B must be on the same device")
   216	
   217	        A = A.contiguous()
   218	        B = B.contiguous()
   219	        C = torch.empty((N, N), device=A.device, dtype=torch.bfloat16)
   220	        gemm_kernel[lambda: ((N // BLOCK_N, N // BLOCK_M, 1), (BLOCK_THREADS, 1, 1))](A, B, C)
   221	        return C

codex
The mismatch is from the initial B LDS staging path: wave ownership was missing on stage 0, so waves were aliasing each other before the pipeline started. I’m fixing that one offset and rerunning.

+

+        a_base1 = even_stage + (wave_id * 64 + a_row + 32) * 4 + a_half * 2

+        a_smem[a_base0 + 1] = a_next_even_words[1]
+        a_smem[a_base1] = a_next_even_words[2]
+        a_smem[a_base1 + 1] = a_next_even_words[3]
+        b_lane_base = (even_stage // 4) + wave_id * 64 + b_quarter * 32 + b_col_frag * 8
+        for s in S.range(4):
+            b_smem_bf16[b_lane_base + s, b_dst_idx] = b_next_even_vals[0, s, 0]

+    even_stage = (final_pair & 1) * LDS_STAGE_WORDS
+    odd_stage = even_stage ^ LDS_STAGE_WORDS

+    b_odd_vals = S.view(b_odd_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+

The simplest path to a correct pipelined kernel here is to keep the original per-tile staging exactly intact and make the double buffering more conservative. I’m removing the intra-tile interleave and keeping the 2-tile software pipeline structure.

Substrate: Using AmdgpuDriver (available: ['AmdgpuDriver', 'NvidiaDriver'])
[Profiling] Using timing method: cudagraph

codex
I found the logic bug: with this 2-tile pipeline, even K-tiles always live in stage 0 and odd K-tiles always live in stage 1. I had incorrectly toggled stage ownership by pair, which corrupts the entire pipeline after the first iteration.
apply patch
patch: completed

Implemented the round-2 kernel in [output_model_new.py](/workspace/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb1/p01/optimization_rounds/round2/output_model_new.py). The kernel keeps the required 4-wave MFMA mapping, stages A/B through LDS, and now uses a 2-tile software pipeline with double buffering and a K-loop unrolled by 2.

Validation passed with the exact required command. The round-local debug result in [debug_eval.jsonl](/workspace/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb1/p01/optimization_rounds/round2/debug_eval.jsonl) shows `correctness: true` and `runtime_us: 14.4`.
